INNER JOIN [sys].[columns] [c] ON [d].[parent_column_id] = [c].[column_id] AND [d].[parent_object_id] = [c].[object_id]
WHERE ([d].[parent_object_id] = OBJECT_ID(N'[phases]') AND [c].[name] = N'UpdatedAt');
IF @var4 IS NOT NULL EXEC(N'ALTER TABLE [phases] DROP CONSTRAINT [' + @var4 + '];');
